Story coming November 5 2023 ________________________________________ Chapter 4: Clearing The Air, Ain't It Gramps ________________________________________ Naruto: The Renegade ________________________________________ Chapter I Cleaning The Air Ain't It Gramps ________________________________________ In Istanbul Turkey, At 7 am a black sedan is moving on the road in which there are three passengers, a man and 2 children who looked like they were going to school. At Istanbul Public School's front gate, the car suddenly stopped, out of the car came a tall blond man about 6'7", looking in his early twenties, and two children, a boy, and a girl. The girl had sun-kissed blond hair with auburn strands of hair in between, had silver eyes shining like the moon while the boy had auburn hair with blond strands and his eyes were that of blue color just like the man behind him. The distinguishable feature about the three of them was the whisker-like marks on their cheek, while both the kids had 2 on each side; the adult had 3 on each side. "Okay, kids go to school and remember no mischief, okay, be good kids and we will go somewhere special." The blond man said. "Really?!" The kids asked in excitement. "Yes, now go Dhriti, Vassilis. Bye." The man said to the kids. "Bye Dad." Both of them replied. "Oh hey, Nakul. Dropping your kids off." Another man asked, now named Nakul. "Yeah, Benji. Okay then, see you later." Nakul said while leaving "Bye Nakul" "Bye Benjamin" As he dropped his kids off at school Nakul Sachdeva went directly to his workplace. Nakul is a hardworking Indian NRI in Turkey, though most people who meet him get thrown off by his blond hair since it's rare to impossible for an Indian to have blonde hair unless it is dyed but Nakul was one of a kind. He works in a software firm as a senior manager, which is remarkable given his age. As for his family, he is an orphan and has a wife and two kids- Dhriti and Vassilis, Vassilis's name was that due to his mother. Since Nakul married a Greco-American woman named Luna and she gave birth to twins, it was decided that she would name one kid while he would name the other. In all, he had a happy family even though sometimes his wife goes abroad for work. After work he went to school to pick his kids up, now obviously he had to finish his work at the office but the head there was so impressed by the work that he gave him the ability to leave the office anytime but he had to finish his work at home which surprisingly he did. Once he left the office drove to the school to pick his kids up. "Daddy!" "Dad!" exclaimed both the kids, happy to see their father. "Ha-ha so how are my kids doing? Been good kids right?" "Yeah" was the answer he got. "So as promised we will be going to the Gulhane's!" "Really!" "Yes!" "Yahoo!" the kids exclaimed in happiness, well since they were big meat connoisseurs and loved their grandaunt's cookies, two traits they seemingly got from their mother. After coming out from the restaurant, they went grocery shopping with the kids. He made this a habit so that the kids knew what was on the menu and there was no excess food made. Once done with the dinner he got his kids off the TV and then sent them to bed. After that, he went into the kitchen and opened a small fridge; he took out a beer bottle from there and started to drink it on the table while thinking about what his wife was doing in the US. At that moment, while drinking he again went into the cabinet and took out another bottle opened it, and kept it on the table. "You know, you were never good at hiding, god knows how you became a spymaster Jiraiya-sama." He said in a whisper. At that moment a man suddenly appeared from the corner of the room. "You know you hurt me by saying Jiraiya-sama, and I thought my apprentice would finally call me sensei," Jiraiya said in a fake hurt tone "Well with an irresponsible man who leaves a baby to an old geezer who couldn't do shit to protect him and another man who neglected him, I don't think so," Nakul replied in a cold tone "Now Naruto..." While Jiraiya was trying to explain to Nakul now named Naruto, in his mind, only one thing was going on. "Shit! The House has been compromised and has to move. New York! Before that, I need to stall for time, so that I have backup. " Naruto was not an idiot to fight him there knowing that even if he had more power the level of experience would make him lose. Simply putting it was like comparing a nuke to a little firecracker "Save your excuses, why are you here? Let me guess, the village wants their precious weapon back. Isn't that right?" Naruto said in a cold tone. "No Naruto it's not like that..." Jiraiya tried to explain to him, but he was rudely cut off by Naruto "Really how is it then? Me acting like an idiot, acting like I had a crush on that banshee, who used me like a punching bag, or acting like the dead last so everyone can laugh at me." "Naruto, people have changed, they have realized what they did and are apologetic for it." Jiraiya tried to explain the situation to him but Naruto was in no mood. "Oh really? Bet it wouldn't be because someone told them about my heritage and are now willing to lick my ass to get in my good graces. Tell you what, give me a good reason I should come back and I will." "Naruto you have your parentage there-" Jiraiya started but was again cut off by Naruto's laugh. "Don't give me that shit Jiraiya, that is the worst excuse I have heard, parentage, parentage right so tell me if I would stay there, would you have given me that? Huh?" Jiraiya was going to reply but Naruto replied for him. "Let me give you the answer, It is once I matured right? Or let's go with once I became Jounin, which was never going to happen with those people there!" "Naruto it's not like that" "Oh it is like that, just because you don't want to leave your delusional bubble does not mean others can" "Fine, let's just talk civilly, look I know we have differences and problems but please let's talk civilly." Jiraiya pleaded with him. Seeing the desperation on Jiraiya's face Naruto relented. "Ok, let's do it, no shouting, nothing, deal," Naruto replied. "Ok" "Look Naruto I know I messed up, Minato, Kushina wanted me to take care of you and we did not. look I messed up and I am sorry for that." Jiraiya said in a heavy tone. Here Naruto caught something. "What do you mean 'we'?" Naruto asked. Knowing that he slipped up Jiraiya knew he had to tell the truth. "Look Naruto, what I am going to say is a secret that only a sensei, me, Tsunade, and your parents, knew. And Tsunade was completely innocent in it." Jiraiya explained while stressing on the last part. "Fine" "Look, It is in the second war that, it happened, after a battle, me and Tsunade got drunk heavily one night, next day to what we know, we woke up together, and then a few days after we found out she was pregnant and-" "You are my grandfather and she is my grandmother." Naruto finished Jiraiya's story in a cold and calm tone which frightened him to a high degree, since the Naruto he knew would have shouted and screamed but he did not. "So dear grandfather tell me, how is she, my dearest grandmother innocent in it?" Naruto asked while Jiraiya cringed at the way he said, grandfather and grandmother. "The day of the attack, she got a false letter from sensei telling her that you did not survive the attack," Jiraiya said to which Naruto again completed him, "Let me guess the letter was from Danzo bla-bla-bla." This shocked Jiraiya as he didn't expect Naruto to know this. "How did you-" "That son of a bitch and his two sidekicks are the bloody reason for basically all of my life sufferings." Naruto interrupted him. "That being said, I'm fine with a civil conversation, no jutsus and no tricks," Naruto said in finality and stood up to activate some seals, which Jiraiya identified as silencing seals. "Seals huh" He said in an impressed tone. "Nine years without someone trying to sabotage or manipulate you gives you a lot of inside in your own life." Jiraiya slightly winced at that, knowing about the blonde's dark childhood. "So, married huh?" Jiraiya continued the small talk. "Yeah, the best thing I have done so far." "Her name?" "Luna" 'That's a beautiful name' Jiraiya thought. "So where and when did you meet?" "Here, about thirteen or so years ago" "Are you happy with your life?" Now this shocked Naruto knowing how stubborn Jiraiya was, but what his tone and facial expression contained was nothing but acceptance. "Yeah" "That's good..." "What?" He asked Naruto as he saw the look Naruto was giving him "You're fine with it? Really?" "What so just because I didn't see you and was a bad grandparent doesn't mean I don't know that you are content with your life or not." Jiraiya replied and then he enquired, "Any kids yet?" "Yeah, twins." "So what are their names?" "Dhriti and Vassilis" "Huh?" "What?" "Thought you would give some traditional names" "We both chose the names, she chose the boy's name and I the girl's." "Oh" "So what about their mother" "Went out of the country for some work" "Oh," Jiraiya said and then he continued "They would have been proud." This brought Naruto's attention. "Would they be?" he said in a whispering tone. "You know they named you after my book that was the worst selling, when Kushina heard about it she had her doubts but Minato convinced her." Jiraiya chuckled wistfully "I still remember the day Kushina announced she was pregnant, I hadn't seen Minato so much happier in his life, not even when they were getting married. For them you were everything." While Jiraiya was recalling the past events, what Naruto saw was no Jiraiya of the Sannin, of the legendary trio who triumphed in hundreds of battles in the second and third shinobi wars. He saw a man who lost everything he cherished and now reminiscing about it. "And then there was that time when your gender was revealed, she was so excited that she even exclaimed, she quote unquote will keep any hussies from sinking their claws, and then she suddenly exclaimed about grandchildren." "Would they have been proud of me?" He asked whisperingly "Oh trust me both of them would have been over the moon to see both of them," Jiraiya said boisterously, making Naruto smile knowing that his parents would have been happy and proud of his life decisions. For an orphan like him, it is the best thing one can say to them that their parents were proud of them. For them it was worth everything, very few could understand the pain that he felt. He would compare the things he went through, the emotional pain, to what Itachi Uchiha felt. "You know when the twins were born, it was both a very frightful yet joyous day of my life, and I thought I lost Luna that day." Naruto started opening up "We were both madly in love, well actually not from the beginning, she was kind of a feminist, you know the ones saying all males are rapists and all, at first I thought she was being a brat but as time passed we fell in love." He mirthfully chuckled "I was nearly out of my wits when she first told me that she was pregnant, I fainted," he said as he recalled that day "When she was seven months in I proposed to her, she almost thought that it was because of the pregnancy, then that delivery date I almost lost her but she pulled through, nowadays these five are my life." "Five?" Jiraiya enquired Naruto then realized his slip of the tongue, but he knew it was too late to cover up so he told the truth. "When I left the hidden lands I washed up on the shores of a country there I met an old lady who took care of me and also has a sister who is an orphan so took her in." "So what are their names?" "Dhriti and Shrishti, Shrishti is my sister's name while the old lady was Dhriti." "So named after her huh." "Yeah, she died, so I thought to name her after the person who showed me what life is." "So, you live with your sister or ..." "No, she goes out for higher studies so stays out but we are in touch." Jiraiya nods at that "So how is she doing?" "After your abandonment, she is a bit worse but her health is fine she even now started taking work seriously." Naruto nods at that and then says, "That's good for her." Jiraiya now was losing on topics to keep the conversation going, he finally asked the unsaid question. "Are you ever planning on returning to the village?" Jiraiya enquired in a grave tone letting Naruto know that he was completely serious and in no mood for joking. "No" Naruto curtly replied and then Jiraiya asked, "Why?" "Jiraiya, if it was only about me then the conversation wouldn't have been on a dining table over two cans of beer, it would have been in a park where we tried to kill each other." Jiraiya somewhat expected this answer from Naruto after conversing with him, but Naruto was not finished, "now, I have lived with me that matter to me the most, people who see the real me not the son of their esteemed yondaime hokage and before you say how at least I have a tenant who reveals things to me like my mother was the last jinchuuriki and as for my father I figured out about it when I was five surprising the village couldn't. Now as I was saying I have people who see me as 'Naruto Uzumaki' not 'Namikaze Naruto' or 'The Fox Brat' or their precious weapon. Going there is borderline suicide for me and I don't want to jeopardize their lives over the petty feuds of the villages." After the mini rant, Naruto took a deep breath to calm himself down and waited for Jiraiya's reply, he honestly thought that it would be on the lines of Jiraiya giving him some patriotic answer but his answer shocked Naruto. "Okay that's fine" "Huh?!" "What? It's your decision, if you're happy then I am fine with it." "So like no patronizing speech?" "No." "Okay well, thanks for understanding." "Hey, that's what older mature people do, we worry for the younger." "Yeah right, you mature, then Konoha loves Kyuubi no Kitsune." "Hey I will tell you I am mature" "Yeah right!" Naruto snorted out and both of them started laughing. Then Jiraiya said, "Hey, thanks for cleaning the air between us." To which Naruto replied, "No, thank you, you know when all this happened in a part of my mind there was always the part that was guilty of leaving the village, leaving what was once my parents' home. Today after learning about them I think I can leave that guilt behind." To which Jiraiya laughed and said, "Oh, no your parents are one of a kind. They will always be happy to know that you are happy regardless of what you do. For them if you loved to do something then they would have allowed you to do that, they once even said that if you did not want to be a shinobi they wouldn't have forced you". This moved Naruto to tears to know that his parents considered this much for him. "Hey thanks, Jiraiya, I appreciate it. Oh, by the way, there is something you might want to hear." "What?" "There is something I can only tell you and Tsunade." This got Jiraiya's attention as Naruto was serious here. "What?" Naruto first did a chakra scan then in a serious voice he answered the question, "Those three old bats might try something to take the Hokage seat and give it to Danzo, map each of your steps and make sure not to do something that might bite you in the back." This confused Jiraiya as he knew about the elders and their mentality. "What do you exactly mean?" Naruto sighed and then said, "That Cyclops was planning something when I underwent the operation, and I heard him planning something with his sidekicks. I don't exactly know what they were planning but it was something that is regarding the Jinchuurikis and the Uzumakis. So, I knew it was dangerous living there and they mentioned you two too." Now this alerted Jiraiya, knowing that those old bags were trying to do something with jinchuurikis is a big red alert but Naruto was not done "Also you should advise Tsunade-sama to investigate the civilian council, those motherfuckers have done a lot of fund embezzlement, you would want to check, during the geezers period most of the powers were in the hands of the council so corruption was at an all-time high and also you might want to check all the shinobis that were charged because some were falsely charged too." "Hey, how do you know so much about the village?" Jiraiya questioned him, to which he gave a cryptic reply, "Sometimes it's good to have eyes and ears inside rather than having them outside." Which Jiraiya instantly knew, meant that he also had a spy ring inside the elemental nations. "Naruto, by the way, what level of sealing are you at?" "Ten, why?" Jiraiya felt a lot of pride and a bit of envy surge through him knowing that his grandson had surpassed him in sealing. So, he reached out of his pants pocket and brought a scroll out. "This is yours now." Naruto curiously and cautiously stared at the scroll. "Your parents always thought about the future so, they also prepared some gifts for your marriage consider this as your wedding gift from us." And then he produced another scroll which when Naruto saw, he nearly gouged his eyes out, as it was labeled 'Hiraishin-no-justu', his father's fabled jutsu, that destroyed a whole battalion of ninjas in a matter of seconds thus giving him the name 'Konoha-no-kiroi-senko'. "This is something Minato wanted to give you as a coming-of-age gift, it's yours now." Then he gave Naruto a picture of them, which had him, Tsunade, Minato, and Kushina, and another of when Kushina was in her seventh month of pregnancy. These drove Naruto to tears as they were something that he would cherish forever. "Hey wait here for a second" Then Naruto went inside his room and brought a picture of him, Luna, and the Twins, "She might want to see them so here you go." When he went over the picture of his grandson, and great-grandchildren, and then his eyes hovered over his grand-daughter in law and said, "She is a beauty" to which Naruto replied, "Yeah, she is my heart." Then Jiraiya stood up and said, "Well would you look at the time, now good sir I will take my leave." Jesting a bit with Naruto as he good-heartedly chuckled and then said, "It was good to see you too gramps, take care and tell Tsunade and Shizune I said hi." To which Jiraiya nodded and said, "Will do." With that Jiraiya went up in smoke. Then Naruto had a question in his mind "How the hell did he find me?" but it was too late to ask the question. "Well time to deal with the other unwanted guests," Naruto said as he sighed and stood up then went to his room, in his closet, and took out a black tuxedo and wore it along with that he took a katana and a shotgun along with ammo. "Well let's get the show on the road." With that, he went outside his house while barrier-sealing it. He didn't have to go very far as in the nearby park from what he estimated about thirty-five to forty people were there. They were wearing the same uniform that is ANBU black pants along with a gray color vest with a blank mask alerting Naruto that it was the ROOT – Danzo's goon army as he called it, since there were no real deadly shinobi in it. In Naruto's own words, it was a cheap copy of ANBU black ops. "Namikaze-sama, we would like you to come with us peacefully." One of the agents standing in front said in a monotone voice. Naruto was having nothing of it, he figured out by sensing that more than half of the are ready with ninjutsu of all five elements some of them with kekkei genkai no wonder since he was a brawler in the past thus overwhelming him, then there were some with genjutsu, that also due to him being awful with that and some them with fuinjutsu, that put a nail in the coffin since, he figured out their motive, if not done peacefully kill him, take the beast, open the barrier, take his children. So he knew one thing for sure, he would be bathing in blood again. "So let me get this straight I have got two options here right? One. I come with you peacefully. Two. You kill me." The ROOT agent nodded, finding no reason to lie about option two. But then they suddenly tensed, sensing Naruto building up chakra, "How about option three where I escort you all to hell." With that, all hell broke loose as Naruto charged towards them. Taking down the first two with a wind-laced Spartan kick piercing and killing them, then he ducked avoiding the two fire justu coming at him, and then himself fired an earth jutsu: Earth style: Dirt Rampart, five of the root agents got killed as the earth beneath them open up and spikes came out of it. Then he did a lightning jutsu frying three more assailants. The ROOT then sent their sealing team, one agent tried the Five pronged seal on him trying to seal his chakra but Naruto saw it way earlier thus twisting his body then he sliced off the agent's wrist followed by slicing off his head. After which he wove the signs for a Fire Style: Dragon Flame Breath killing the rest six of the sealing squad. After this, he caught three other agents in Water Style: Water Prison the water being produced from the air around them, and electrocuted them with Lightning Style: Electromagnetic Murder. Then he threw off the nine of them with a Wind Style: Great Breakthrough. "Now the real fun begins", he dashed off with lightning chirping in his hands. He slices off one of the agents' heads with his hand and then the color of the lightning suddenly changed to red and with it made a long stick that pierced the incoming agent's chest, then it changed its color to purple as Naruto forced his hand diagonally through another assailants armpits slicing towards the neck and then the lightning's color changed to white as in a swift motion his hand moved from the dead agents chest to slicing the incoming agents jugular. As the agent slowly died the lightning turned its color into pitch black while he shoved his hands into another assailant's chest and then he intensified the lightning frying the agent from inside. Then the lightning disappeared from his hands and became black due to being coated with steel, which was found out as an agent raised his tanto to kill Naruto but Naruto broke the blade by stopping it with his arm. Then he grabbed the man's head and created a vacuum field around it, effectively suffocating him. The rest of the three were killed like they were just cannon fodder. He passed through them with two diagonal slashes and a stab all the while the captain stood there still, the last agent hoped their captain would help them but they were so engrossed in following orders that they didn't know that their captain was trapped in a subtle but effective genjutsu. So, in his last ditch effort before his dying breath, he undid the genjutsu on their captain which Naruto got the wind of, and immediately stood in front of the captain. Then as he came to his senses he saw Naruto standing in front of him and he immediately looked left and right all he saw were the corpses of his comrades, of which some were burned, some wet, some pierced, some slashed and one had his tanto broken and was dead. Then he moved his head towards Naruto hearing the sound of whistling and then he saw Naruto whistle and his head moving downward as if motioning him to do that also. When he did that blood splashed and his vision went blurred till it was pitch black. It turns out that another Naruto beheaded him. They nodded towards each other and then the original went back towards their house while the other went towards the clean-up job. What both of them did not notice was a bird with a scroll flying away and a plant-like creature sinking into the earth. Once Naruto reached the house he dialed a number, and the call was accepted. "Hello", said a female voice from the receiver's end. "Hey, how are you?" "Fine, why? Mr tough Guy is sounding worried my god!" She said with a voice laced with amusement. "They found us." "Them!" She was shocked "Yes" "So what are you going to do now?" She said in a serious voice "Artemis, I don't know, I don't want our kids' future to suffer due to my matter." "Naru I know you are worried but I am not going to help us in the long run, for now, be positive, where is the hubby I know and love gone?" "He is right now at home, packing, ready to go to the US and meet a certain woman." "Oh really! And pray to tell what the woman looks like?" "She has a sexy ass along with auburn hair and the most beautiful pair of silver eyes that shine like the moon in the night sky." "Don't flatter me, idiot! We already have two kids, want to make a third one?" "Nope, these two are already troublesome, and do not want another one." "Hey, they are our kids" With that they both started laughing. "Okay bye, I still have to pack." "Fine, I will receive you at the airport, bye love you." "Love you too." As the call disconnected he started thinking about his journey till now, how he came to these lands, how he met the man-hating goddess, how they fell head over heels for each other, and how they married and had kids. Meanwhile in Konohagakure no Sato A lady with blonde hair and honey-brown eyes was sitting behind a desk doing paperwork. Tsunade Senju, fifth hokage of Konohagakure no Sato, was doing her paperwork and lamenting about her favorite blonde, regret is what was filling her. All what ifs, if she didn't read the letter, if she stayed in the village and all others of them. She wanted a ray of hope so she sent Jiraiya out of the continent which was forbidden or more of an unwritten rule hoping he could give her some good news. "Tsunade-sama" She was brought out of her thoughts by another lady who had shoulder-length black hair and was carrying a pig with her who had a pearl necklace around its neck. "Shizune," the now-named Shizune said, "Milady there is more paperwork I am keeping them there." Seeing that she was not listening, Shizune sighed, "You are thinking about him aren't you." To this, Tsunade gave a melancholic smile and said, "It has been sixteen years since he is gone. How do you think he is doing?" "I honestly don't know if Tsunade-sama, we even know he is alive or not." Tsunade immediately responded to the comment by saying, "No, he is very much alive, Shizune, he is too stubborn to die." Shizune saw her master's eyes filled with stubbornness so she didn't pry too much and said, "Hope Jiraya-sama can bring in some good news." "Did someone take my name!" a boisterous voice came from the window, "Jiraiya-sama!" Shizune cried in shock, while Tsunade sighed and said "Well, speak of the idiot and the idiot appears." Jiraiya dramatically whined and said, "Hime that was mean!" Tsunade just rolled her eyes at her old teammate's dramatics, "So any news?" "Well there is but, there are too many people in the room," Jiraya said in a serious tone. Shizune and the ANBU guards got the memo and quietly left the room. Then Jiraiya suddenly took out four kunais and threw them in the four corners of the office and suddenly four hidden agents were killed and their bodies instantly burned, "Danzo" Tsunade venomously said, "So what is the news." After making sure they were not being spied on he said "There is good news and bad news." Tsunade raised her eyebrows and urged him to continue, "The good news is that when I went outside the continent I went to a place where I found Nine-Tails fresh chakra meaning he is alive and doing well." Before Tsunade could say anything Jiraiya continued "But I wouldn't go and search for him right now." As she dozed off she had a divine dream, "Dhriti my daughter" Shiva started while Dhriti expected him to be disappointed not doing her job. "I am very proud of you" "My lord you are-. Huh, what?!" "I said, I am proud of you" "So you are not disappointed with me for not waiting" Shiva nodded while she was doing a victory dance like a child would do when they are not scolded but praised for something. Shiva chuckled at the display "Now, now easy Dhriti" Shiva lightly chided while she had an embarrassed blush on her cheeks Shiva continued, "I have come to congratulate you on your recent achievement, not only you have brought the champion to safety, but but passed the test." Dhriti nodded to this that her assumption was correct on the champion thing but then something that Shiva said felt weird "My lord what do you mean by me passing the test?" "Oh we give tests to every champion and caretaker of the champion to see their morality, should you have not taken care of him you would have failed the test," Shiva stated while Dhriti nodded. "My daughter guides him. Guide him towards the path of righteousness." Shiva said. "I will my lord," Dhriti said as Shiva left her dream giving her the rest required for her. As the night passed she woke up the next morning with a bit of sore back. When she woke up she saw that Abhijit was walking up the hallway towards the room, "Is he fine?" "Slept all night without any complexion, surprisingly high rate of recovery so you can take him by afternoon." He said. "Okay, then get him ready." While this all was happening in the patient's room Naruto was slowly waking up. His whole body was sore to say the least, thinking only one thing why was he getting such comeuppance? What has he done wrong? "So you finally woke up brat," Kyuubi said in his mind. This made Naruto open his senses a bit more, "Hey Kyuubi where are we?" "Don't know Brat wherever we are it is not the elemental nations. It seems we cross the veil." Kyuubi said, "What veil, what are you talking about?" Naruto asked "Nothing! Forget about anything I said. All I can say right now is that we are in some other part of the world and it is not in elemental nations." Kyuubi said while thinking "The brat needs not to know about the veil right now. When the time comes and if it comes then I will tell him." As the fox thought, Naruto was trying to move every muscle of his body, trying his level best but to no avail. Then he saw in his blurred vision two people walking into his room, he wanted to ask them where he was but felt extreme fatigue from even opening his mouth, then one of them approached him and said something he could not understand as if they were speaking a different language. From what he could gather the person was a female and her words were very soothing along with the head caressing, she made him sleep instantly once again. Dhriti when entered the room, she saw Naruto stirring up so she went to him, knowing the extent of the injury she soothed him by telling him to go to sleep. Abhijit was there standing by the door staring at the old woman, he had never seen such maternal love, since her son's death. He knew that the child was someone from her family but the question begged who? "Dida I wanted to know, if it is not too personal. What is his relation to you?" Abhijit asked curiously, which put Dhriti in a bind. If she did not answer the question it would arouse suspicion in their mind so she had to think up on a quick and a good lie. So she started her melodramatic sob story in her way to divert the attention from people. "He is my grandson." She said in a manner that was like dropping a bombshell. The reaction was as expected Abhijit's eyes widened and mouth agape, "How?" was his only question. "Well, when a man and a woman-" Dhriti began but Abhijit cut her off, "I know that but I am asking how? He has blonde hair and as far as I can remember neither your son nor your daughter-in-law had blonde hair." The only response he got was "He is my grandson, nothing more, nothing less." The Abhijit what she meant and asked, "Illegitimate?" and he got a nod as his answer, confirming his suspicions but he did not pry further due to the amount of respect for the woman he had, as someone who set his career as a doctor from a petty thief in his teens. "So when can I take him home?" She asked him. "In about an hour." She nodded at that response. As an hour passed, she was still outside Naruto's room. Abhijit then came to her, "Okay he is ready for the release, we will get him in a wheelchair and you can take him home." Then a team of nurses came inside the room and manhandled him to get him into the wheelchair as that happened he was finally brought out of the room, he was, in a semi-conscious state almost looking like a zombie with his pale complexion. Dhriti took him in his wheelchair and then moved him towards the gate of the hospital. As they were moving him not many people queried about Naruto since they had seen her in the Hospital quite often, helping random patients sometimes bringing them to a taxi, escorting them to their houses. So they thought it was the same for this person too. Then Abhijit called a taxi and stopped it, the driver peeks out of the window and asks, "Where?" then Abhijit said "Army Lady's house" and the driver nodded. This was one beauty about West Bengal, if you are renowned in your area then every other locomotive driver would know your house, and the locality is like family, so they would know everything about your home and family and all the family becomes relatives to the point the kids call the adults, Uncle and Aunty while the Elderly grandpa and grandma. So when the taxi arrived there along with Naruto in it everyone was curious as to who had come into her home. Then she took him inside the house, on the ground floor inside a room, she had already a guest room ready so it was not an issue, then he was dismantled from the wheelchair and onto the bed then let him rest as sleep took over him, then she went to satisfy the quires of the locality. One thing that was odd about Dhriti's house was that, though being in her late 50's she did not have any house help. One thing she always insisted on was not having any house help. She always said that she did not want any help until she had kicked the bucket or had some illness. So till then, she wanted to do everything on her own. However, from time to time, some people from her locality insist on helping her out of their admiration and respect for her. So after she had settled some queries of the locality by stating that Naruto was a friend's son who had paralysis, she went home. And locality bought it since she had a lot of foreign friends, so having a cripple son of a friend in her house was not a problem. Dhriti entered her house and after freshening up she went into Naruto's room, where he was still sleeping. She gave him saline water while giving him a massage to relax his muscles which was contracted beyond belief. And then gave him acupuncture to restore the muscles, as this was going on Naruto who was in a semiconscious state was feeling relaxed like never before. It was like heaven on Earth for him. After a week of the same treatment for him, the saline water, massage, and acupuncture. His face was now regaining color while the muscles were relaxing a lot, which gave Dhriti a glimmer of hope that he was recovering. During this period she also got a feeling, she had long since forgotten. Caring for him had awakened the feeling of maternal love. Her only granddaughter was sent to a boarding school by her, which both of them understood as she wanted some alone time to cope with her parent's death, so she was sent. But she always came here during Durga Puja and Summer Vacation to spend time with her grandmother, a time when both felt happiness in the company of each other. So when she saw Naruto she had one thing in mind, "You work in mysterious ways, my lord. You might be a champion for god but for me, you are not. You might be a warrior, but I will not treat you as one but as my grandson. Thank you, Lord, for giving me the chance." As she said that as if it was like Naruto had listened his facial muscle had turned into a smile, which fluttered Dhriti's heart as she smiled at him with motherly love. This treatment lasted three more days and after ten days, Naruto fully became conscious. The first thing that he saw was the ceiling with something circular that looked like it was rotating (a ceiling fan) that was providing him air. Then the next thing he noticed was that he was on a much more comfortable bed than he had back in the village next thing he saw there was a wooden door in front of him and a glass beside him on his left. "You are still a bit weak so refrain from a lot of movement please." He heard what sounded to be a female speaking something gibberish as he turned around he said. "{Who are you?!}" (please note that { With Italics}means that I am writing Japanese as I do not have the patience or mind to translate English to Japanese, so yeah!) Dhriti first tried to speak with him in English, seeing his blond hair and blue eyes she got the idea he might be from the West. But when she heard him, he was speaking Japanese which was weird for her due to his hair and eye color. The Dhriti with a heavy accent spoke, "{What is your name?}" Naruto was shocked when he heard her, speaking something he could understand. He quickly replied, "{My name is Uzumaki Naruto, what is your name, old lady?}" Dhriti chuckled at the old lady's remark and then she said, "{Well my name is Ghosh Agarwal Dhriti.}" Then he asked, "{Um where are we, old lady?}" "{We are in West Bengal, India}" She replied. "{Where is India, is it in the land of water}" He asked. Being the airhead he is, he forgot that Kyuubi said that they were NOT IN ELEMENTAL NATIONS. Kyuubi hearing the answer face palmed, "Idiot!". "{Land of water?}" "{Land of fire, land of water you know? Elemental nations?}" "{I am sorry my child, but where is elemental nations?}" This shocked Naruto, and then Dhriti walked out of the room leaving him alone. After some time she came with a piece of paper with her, "{Naruto please tell where is elemental nations are on this map.}" As Naruto frantically searched around on the map to find the land he could not find it there, "{It-It is no-not there!}" He said shaking while sobbing a bit thinking about the mess as the situation was a bit to handle. Dhriti seeing this wrapped her arm around the sobbing boy and caressed his hair, "{Shh, it's okay, everything will be fine eventually.}" As his sobbing came to an end, he suddenly asked the question whisperingly, "{Why?}" "{Why what?}" "{Why do you CARE FOR ME?!}" His sudden shout did shock her but the question made her more inquisitive, "{Why should I not care for you?}" "{All of you old people are the same, you all manipulate and use me!}" He snarled still hurt from recent events that happened to him so the trust department was a little- oh well mostly closed for now. When Dhriti heard this all she could think that what kind of life he had to live he was paranoid to this level. While most people would have maintained their distance from him, giving him space unfortunately or fortunately for Naruto Dhriti was a Delhiite, so she would not leave him alone. She would make him he would feel safe and would become a parental figure in his life. During the following days, Naruto was still recovering. While physically he was improving, mentally, the story was very different. The paranoia was on the next level, the first day, he didn't eat at all thinking the food might be adulterated, but in front of food his mental barriers crumbled and he ate, what was a simple fish curry but for him it was simply heaven (shows what hunger can do to people). As all of this was going on, he had a small talk with her. From all the small talk she had with Naruto, she got to know that he was an orphan, and had no relatives, this small piece of information only strengthened the fire of determination to be a strong parental figure for him. It was a way to give the young child a good future and a path of redemption for the failure of the mother she was. The next few days followed the same pattern but this time Naruto was a bit warming up to Dhriti, he was still as cold as he was during meeting her for the first time but had mellowed out a bit with now the answers being one-liners from the past 'hn's. During this time only Dhriti jokingly propped a question to get a reaction from Naruto "{Will you be my grandson?}" Only to get a cold rebuttal in the form of 'No' and 'Forget it' but in all, from Dhriti's point of view, their bonding was beginning. What Dhriti did not know was that tomorrow would be a day she would not forget in her life, a day which would not only skyrocket the bond between her and Naruto but also her chance of redemption and his getting a parental figure will increase. It was a normal morning, nothing out of the usual for anyone. It could be said the same for the Ghosh house too, as Dhriti and Naruto woke up, greeted each other, and then ate their breakfast in relative quietness, a thing that they both appreciated very much. During his stay here Naruto was familiarized with tea, a drink he has quite taken a liking to. During his stay here another thing Naruto now wanted to do was training, so he went to the roof to do that. Since his tenant was still sleeping and recovering he thought to use summons then he remembered one crucial thing he did not have any summons now, his mind was going through one thing what would he do now, then a memory popped up in Naruto's mind. It was off when he and Jiraiya went to retrieve Tsunade, that time while they were resting near a shrine, Jiraiya told him about his team meeting and test, at least Sarutobi Hiruzen was a competent teacher that Hatake Kakashi, he could not help but give a jab towards his so-called sensei. When he hears those stories from Jiraiya, he remembers how Jiraiya got his summons, it was not through a summoning scroll but by doing the hand signs to check which clan he has an affinity towards. So taking a page from Jiraiya's life he started doing the same thing knowing this could be very dangerous but then again his name was Uzumaki Naruto. While doing the hand signs for the summoning jutsu, he chanted only one thing in his mind "Not the toads" because he knew that if he popped up on Mount Miyoboku his life would be, in short words, fucked, completely fucked. Since the toads were allied to Jiraiya and Jiraiya to Konoha using Euclid's Axiom (not that Naruto knew about Euclid or his Axioms) Toads were allied to Konoha. So if he reached there he would very well get deported to Konoha making his escape a big fail. With that in mind he drew his blood required for summoning and then went through the hands signs Boar Dog Bird Monkey Ram (in order), then slammed his hands to the ground while saying 'summoning jutsu' which is where a seal matrix appeared and in a he disappeared. As this happened Naruto had still one thing in mind 'NOT THE TOADS', once he reappeared somewhere the smoke cleared and he was in some kind of a jungle. As the smoke cleared it was more obvious he was in a jungle. Without much in his mind, he went forward exploring the jungle. One thing that was very peculiar for him about the jungle is its uncanny resemblance with the training ground 44 also known as the forest of death or Anko's stomping grounds in his village. Keeping the thoughts aside he went deep inside the forest and was thankful about not having giant bugs or rouge snakes in the jungle as the events of chuunin exams resurfaced in his mind, causing an involuntary shudder. As he was going inside the forest he saw a quicksand. Looking towards the center of the quicksand, a small indent on the surface of the quicksand made him realize whoever it was, was already drowning in the sand and would meet their death in a matter of moments. It felt scared and helpless and Naruto had to help whatever it was. By channeling the chakra at the bottom of his feet Naruto ran across the quicksand towards its center and channeled the chakra into his arms to give him more strength before he put his hands into the quicksand and wrapped around whoever was sinking. With great strength, he fought against the quicksand and pulled whoever it was out. He stumbled back a little and landed on his butt. He took a deep breath since he had to use more strength than he thought he would against the quicksand, something many shinobi hated since there were very few ways to get out of it. Whoever it was in the quicksand was very small, so small in fact that if he squeezed them any tighter then they might have popped. He looked down to see the person he just saved. Though who he saved was not a person at all. Looking down he saw it was a small cat, so tiny in fact that he could probably put her on top of his head. The little cat was completely white and had black stripes all over its body. Its paws were tiny, almost as tiny as a baby's hand. A pair of sharp teeth was protruding from its mouth. "Hey there little guy. What are you doing in a big scary place like this?" He said as the little cat opened its eyes to reveal big green eyes looking back at him with a cat slit-like pupil looking back at him. It stared at him for a moment before it let out a small meow and licked his cheek affectionately making him laugh a little. "HA HA that tickles little fella." He said as he patted its head. "Thanks, you mister. I thought I was going to die." The little cat said making Naruto look at it in surprise. "You talk?" He asked as it bopped its head up and down. "Yuh huh of course I talk." "Wells that's pretty cool. I have never met a talking cat before. Talking toads and slugs yes but never a little cat." He guessed he said something wrong because the little cat began hitting its tiny paws against him while it made a facial expression that he guessed was a pout. "I'm not a cat you big dummy. I'm a tiger, a white tiger from the White Tiger clan. And stop calling me fella, I'm a girl." The little tiger revealed making Naruto look at her in surprise. "Oh well, I am sorry about that." He said before he put his hand out to her. "My name is Naruto. It's nice to meet you." He said as the little tiger cub looked at him with her big green eyes before she copied his motions and placed her paw on top of his hand. "My name is Kohaku, part of the White Tiger Clan." She said as Naruto nodded and stood he walked away from the quicksand with Kohaku still in his arms. He held her close so that she did not fall back into the quicksand and he gently stroked her beautiful coat of fur, removing bits of sand from it as he did. "You know I don't think I have ever heard of a White Tiger Clan before," Naruto said. "I am aware of the Toads, Snakes, Slugs, Monkeys, and Dogs but White Tigers are a new one to me." Kohaku moved her little head to look up at him. "Kaa-san doesn't like our kind going out in the world too much. She says long ago people killed the small Tigers for sport and lots of us died. So Kaa-san wants us to stay in our homeland since it is safe there and no one can hurt us." Naruto smiled. "Your Kaa-san sounds very smart and she sounds like she cared a lot for her family." Kohaku bobbed her head. "She is and she is very powerful. Kaa-san is the chief of the White Tiger Clan. A lot of the other Tigers are a little scared of her since she is very strong. But I think Kaa-san is a big softie." 'Yeah, I bet.' Naruto thought. "If you are not allowed usually allowed to leave your home then why are you in this forest?" He asked. Kohaku gave him a very toothy smile. "Kaa-san says I'm a very curious child and I always want to see what's outside of home. But Kaa-san likes it when I'm close by since I am Mama's only cub." "So she's very protective over you." He said as Kohaku nodded. "Very so she might be a little mad that I am out here," she said before she jumped out of Naruto's arms. "You should meet her. I think she would like you since you saved me!" "I don't think that would be a good idea." He said waving his arms but Kohaku did not listen and placed her paw on the ground in front of them. As she did, a black marking appeared on the ground, and Naruto recognized the summoning seals. A second later a large cloud of smoke appeared and it made Naruto very nervous. He thought the cloud would be small, about a man's size or bigger but instead, it was enormous, covering parts of the forest, and went far over the tops of the trees. 'Oh, crap.' He thought hoping that Kohaku's mother would not turn him into 'cat' food. As the cloud began to disappear, Naruto unconsciously took a step back, and for good reason. The creature in front of him was the very definition of enormous. She towered over the tree's tops and if he had to guess, he would say that she was even bigger than Gamabunta, at least a good head taller. Her fur was like Kohaku's, snow white with long black stripes over her body but her coat had a shine that he guessed came with age. Her eyes were jade green as well and the claws on her paws were even bigger than his mother's. On the top of her head was what looked like some kind of tiara with an emerald in the center of it and her tail and shoulder muscles had this greyish silver armour to it. The enormous White Tiger looked around in confusion. "Where am I?" she called out in a strong but very elegant-sounding voice. The voice had nobility laced all over it. "Kaa-san down here!" Kohaku's squeaky voice called and at first, he wondered if the giant Tiger would even be able to her. But she did when her large head looked down and towards Kohaku. "Kohaku." She said in a stern voice as her head lowered down to the ground to look at her daughter. "What have I told you about leaving Mount Taigahiru? You know I don't like you leaving our home without me knowing or at all." Kohaku stood up on her hind legs, which would have reached to Naruto's knee, against her mother's enormous nose. "But Kaa-san it's so boring at home. And I met a new friend. See?" She said looking over at Naruto whose eyes went a little wide as the enormous eyes of the White Tiger chief moved towards him and narrowed. A deep growl came out of her throat that made the area vibrate and Naruto could feel the hairs on the back of his neck stand up. "Did this person hurt you my little cub?" She asked as the mother Tiger rose to its full height making Naruto wonder if anyone else from the village could see the enormous Tiger since he doubted anyone could ever miss her. Naruto gulped and readied himself to defend himself if possible but Kohaku leaped in front of Naruto and looked at her mother with a pout on her face. "Kaa-san please don't hurt him. He saved me. I might have died if he had not arrived." The great tiger looked a little put back when her daughter spoke before her eyes narrowed again and went back down to look at Kohaku's. "Start explaining daughter," she said though it sounded more like a command. So Kohaku began to explain what had happened, how she fell into quicksand as she chased a butterfly around and drowned in it when Naruto arrived and took her out of the sand before it could completely engulf her. Naruto stood to the side as the mother tiger scolded her little cub for foolish actions before her giant nose touched Kohaku's body. "I thought I might have lost you." She said softly as Kohaku stood on her hind legs again and licked her mother's nose in comfort. Naruto smiled. She is just a mother worried about her child. The giant Tiger moved her head and looked towards Naruto before she stood at her full height again making Naruto take a gulp. No words were spoken momentarily as the mighty White Tiger chief boss looked down at Naruto with her large green eyes gazing right into him. After a moment of silence, she spoke. "Saving my daughter as you did has put you in a favorable light and your actions have gained my thanks, young man. Few would dare to risk saving another from death, less likely counting we are of different species. For saving my daughter, you have my thanks. I am Shirotora, Chief of the White Tiger Clan of Mount Taigahiru." Knowing to be polite in this situation, Naruto bowed to the giant White Tiger leader. "I am Naruto Uzumaki Namikaze. It's nice to meet you." He said as Shirotora nodded to him. "You will have to forgive my earlier rudeness to you young cub, my kind have had bad experiences with humanity so we tend to avoid interaction with them. You are the first human I have spoken to in many decades." "He is real nice Kaa-san. He cleaned me and got rid of the sand." Kohaku said as she showed her mother her clean fur. "It was no problem at all Shirotora-sama. I was just glad that I could help and save your daughter when I did. If not then I dread to think what might have happened." Shirotora nodded her head and was about to speak when Kohaku was waving her paws in the air, trying to get her attention. "Kaa-san we should reward him. I know how we can reward him. It is the best idea I have ever had." She said as Naruto chuckled at the little cub while Shirotora rolled her eyes but smiled a big toothy smile showing her large sharp teeth. "What is your idea young one?" Kohaku gave her a big smile and padded over to Naruto as she rubbed her head against his leg purring before answering. "Let him become our summoner and sign the White Tiger Contract." She said as both Naruto and Shirotora looked at her in surprise. Naruto did not have any words to say though inwardly he was bursting with happiness. He wanted to have summons that were not toads and they were giving him a chance. Shirotora meanwhile narrowed her eyes to look at her daughter and Kohaku. "Kohaku, might I remind you we have never had a summoner before? Why should we start now?" Kohaku frowned. "But Kaa-san this could be a good way to get back into this world, plus Naruto would be a good summoner. Right?" She asked as Naruto quickly nodded his head. Shirotora stood tall as she looked down at Naruto with her piercing green eyes staring intently into him, almost as if she was staring into his very soul and trying to see if he was worthy enough to be their first summoner. "Hmm. Young one come with us to Taigahiru there the real test will commence to see if you are a worthy summoner or not." Then he was again pulled through space and time to a mountain this time it was filled with tigers. As they were they went inside there was a giant cave where the trio entered it. Then as they went inside Shirotora called someone "MA" Naruto now anticipatingly waited for this 'Ma' person, then of one of the gates came a small bipedal tiger with a cane in hand, "Oh! Shiro-chan, Ko-chan!" as she came closer she suddenly left upwards in the air surprising all of them and then suddenly Naruto felt intense pain on his head by a cane and then his vision gradually went black. "Human be gone!" she yelled. "Ma! What the hell?!" Shirotora exclaimed. "What you know, he is a human and you know what humans have done with us don't you" Ma replied. "But he helped me!" Kohaku butted in. This piqued Ma's curiosity. "Explain," She said authoritatively, she might be an old tigress, but she would be damned if tigers did not respect her. Then Kohaku and Shirotora started explaining what happened from Kohaku getting trapped in a quicksand to Shirotora considering him a summoner. "So you want to have him as a summoner" "Yes ma" "Hmm okay Shiro-chan, do not take the second test." "Why Ma?" "He saving Kohaku was enough. Take him to my house I will take the first test and then tell you." After settling him into her house, she made some hand signs with her paws, and then put her hand on his head and closed her eyes after some time Naruto opened his eyes to see the tigress that hit him in front of him. "Ah don't worry Naruto Uzumaki Namikaze, son of Kushina Uzumaki and Minato Namikaze, I mean no harm, Myself Baatora." "Well action speaks louder than words, but did you know about my parents." "Ah, that is due to a jutsu that lets me see your memories. Nifty don't you think?" "What do you exactly want?" "To ask you a simple question?" "Ask away." "If you have a family, a wife, and children and you still lived in Konoha who would you have given preference to." It did not even take Naruto a second before answering, "Family, I am not going to repeat the same mistake made by my father." Baatora got the answer she required. Tigers are a proud clan, pride in always protecting their family and pride in selflessness and bravery, all the qualities this human in front of her had shown so she made her decision. "Child, come with me." As they left the cave, after walking outside they met with the mother-daughter duo, "So ma what is your decision?" Shirotora asked. "Well, how about bring out the summoning scroll sound like?" She asked cheekily, and all of them smiled knowing she passed the test. Shirotora looked down towards Kohaku and gave her a small nod which made the little cub bounce in happiness before she placed her paw on the ground and another poof went out, though this time was only a tiny one. Out of the smoke was a large scroll, about the size of the one Jiraiya carried on his back for the Toads. It was grey and on each end had a silver tiger head while the Kanji for White Tiger was written on the side. "Open it up," Shirotora said to Naruto who quickly nodded and did so. He opened up the scroll to show long empty columns, once again proving that they had never had any summoners before. 'Cool.' He thought as he went down to his knees and looked the scroll over as Kohaku sat beside him and Shirotora looked over him. Then Naruto knew what to do as he took his right thumb and bit into the skin. He saw a tiny bit of blood flow out of the wounds and quickly began to write his name into the scroll. After a few moments, he took his hand away and looked at the scroll that now had his name written in the first column. "And that's it," Shirotora said as the name glowed for a moment before it turned black, now permanently becoming part of the scroll. "You are now officially the first summoner of the White Tiger Summons. Don't disappoint us." She warned as Naruto quickly nodded though he had a big smile plastered on his face. "Kohaku, since this was your idea, you will be the boy's familiar." Kohaku happily nodded before she jumped up and climbed on Naruto until she sat comfortably on his head while an amused Naruto looked up at her. After spending some time there he summoned himself to the house he was living in not before promising Kohaku that he would spend more time with her. (I mean how can someone deny something to such a cute kitty, I am sure will not.) As he reappeared inside the Ghosh House, It had been about 4 to 5 hours in his journey. During that time Dhriti was frantically searching the house and locality while remaining as less suspicious as one could be. Then when she saw Naruto and ran towards him and hugged the life out of him, "{where were you Naruto? Did you know how worried I was?}" She exclaimed. In his usual cold tone he said "{it is none of your business}", this time something snapped in Dhriti, "{none of my business huh, I tore down the whole locality for you and none of my business!}" She raised her voice. This snapped Naruto and in a raised voice he said, "{Why the hell do you care?!}" This enraged Dhriti, "{Why the hell do I care? I saved your life and then nursed it that is why!}" Naruto then replied in a snarky way, "{yeah let me guess! You did it out of pity, poor child no one to care for him, let me do it so he can become eternally grateful about it.}" This comment genuinely hurt Dhriti and it could be seen on her face as she yelled "{go to your room!}" While they separated from each other, they were contemplating their words, Dhriti regretted that she took a hot approach to it while Naruto regretted his words after seeing the genuine hurt on her face. One of them, which caught his eye was 'The Eight Inner Gates'. He had already seen the effectiveness of the said jutsu by Busy Brow and it was extremely effective, so he was excited to learn the eight inner gates. But then he remembered what Tobirama had said to him while in his apprenticeship: ' Before learning a jutsu, know about its drawbacks. No matter how powerful a jutsu maybe it will always have a weakness.' So he started thinking about the drawback of eight inner gates. While reading about the description of the jutsu, found out that it had one simple drawback, the jutsu is mainly taijutsu-based, so if anyone had a strong Ninjutsu defense like Gaara's sand, the jutsu would be effectively useless. Then he had a borderline suicidal idea, that instead of learning the jutsu, he could make a jutsu like the Eight Inner Gates, but instead of only taijutsu, it would be an all-rounder jutsu, which covers all the basic aspects of Shinobi, Ninjutsu, Taijutsu, and Genjutsu as he did with Rasengan. He made Rasenshuriken and Kieru Rasengan (Vanishing Rasengan). So, he started first nitpicking the given jutsu. It took a hell of a lot of time and by the early evening when he decided to return to his apartment, he even hadn't deciphered the intricate details of the First gate but during his month of training, he learned the most important lesson 'patience', thus he decided to give it rest for that day. From the next day, he formed a plan, he would visit various places in Japan, preferably dense forests, to not arouse suspicion. If he went to one forest every day, people might get suspicious about his workings and he might get caught. So he found ten forests to help him in his endeavor. The next morning after a short meeting with Iman he left for Bijinbayashi in Niigita, he booked a hotel for two days to do his research, and his decision did bore fruit as he, in those two days cracked the workings behind the first of the eight inner gates. He found out that the jutsu uses the Chakra to accelerate the body's metabolism and power which results in the Shinobi getting greater strength and stamina for a deathly amount of chakra, thus called a forbidden jutsu. Also, he found out that every gate affected or siphoned chakra from different places. For the first four gates, it was the chakra pool. The next two were from the outer skeletal system, for the seventh, it was from the muscular system, and for the gate of death, was from all over the body, effectively killing the person while giving him or her, an exponential boost of power. After deciphering the theory, he came back to Tokyo, staying in his apartment and researching the theory in detail, it took him a week but he concluded that he would have to go through the dreaded and irritating training of Gensotora. So, the next morning, he left for the island of Kyushu, a place where he could train while keeping track of the veil.
